"anterior chamber and related structures, external approach. this class includes one or more of 24 standard surgical interventions or procedures on component parts of the anterior chamber and related structures with external approach.  these surgical interventions or procedures are listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems or icd-10 pcs under code 08.. .
